    USER: I wrote a sentence in English, but I'm not sure if it's grammatically correct. Here's my sentence: Every student, and he wears socks, is a swinger. 1. Are there any grammar mistakes in my sentence? Yes or No; 2. If yes, what is the category of the mistake: syntax, morphology or semantics ? If there's no mistakes, write 'None'

Yes or No; 2. If yes, what is the category of the mistake: syntax, morphology or semantics ? If there's no mistakes, write 'None'

    2. The category of the mistake is syntax.
    3. Here's the corrected sentence: I asked when we could leave.
EXPLANATION:
The word "inquired" is not incorrect per se, but it is less common and more formal than "asked". Additionally, "when could we leave" should be "when we could leave", as "could" is a modal verb that requires the subject to be in the first person (I/we).
The corrected sentence uses simpler language and correct word order, making it easier to understand.
